	function faderError(){
		this.faderForm = document.forms["faderForm"];
		this.faderDiv = document.getElementById('fader');
		this.faderTable = document.getElementById('faderTable');
		this.cancelButtonStyleRef = document.getElementById('cancelButton');
		this.submitButtonStyleRef = document.getElementById('submitButton');
		this.cancelButtonRef = this.faderForm.elements["cancelButton"];
		this.submitButtonRef = this.faderForm.elements["submitButton"];
		this.setErrorHeader = function(errorHeader){ document.getElementById('errorHeader').innerHTML=errorHeader };
		this.setErrorMessage = function(errorMessage){ document.getElementById('errorMessage').innerHTML=errorMessage };	
		this.showError = function(){ this.faderDiv.style.display=''; this.faderDiv.style.visibility='visible'};
		this.hideError = function(){ this.faderDiv.style.display='none'; this.faderDiv.style.visibility='hidden'};
		// note: submit and cancel button onclick events require a function		
		this.setCancelButtonValue = function(cancelButtonValue){ this.cancelButtonRef.value=cancelButtonValue };
		this.setCancelButtonOnClick = function(cancelButtonOnClick){ this.cancelButtonRef.onclick=cancelButtonOnClick };		
		this.setSubmitButtonValue = function(submitButtonValue){ this.submitButtonRef.value=submitButtonValue };
		this.setSubmitButtonOnClick = function(submitButtonOnClick){ this.submitButtonRef.onclick=submitButtonOnClick };				
		this.hideCancelButton = function(){ this.cancelButtonStyleRef.style.display="none" };		
		this.hideSubmitButton = function(){ this.submitButtonStyleRef.style.display="none" };
		this.setFormAction = function(formAction){ this.faderForm.action = formAction };
		this.setFormOnSubmit = function(formOnSubmit){ this.faderForm.onsubmit = formOnSubmit };
		this.submitForm = function(){ this.faderForm.submit() };
		this.setFaderWidth = function(faderWidth){ this.faderTable.style.width = faderWidth };
		this.setFaderHeight = function(faderHeight){ this.faderTable.style.height = faderHeight};
	}
</script>

	/*
	function toggleFaderDiv(divID,forceLeftSep,forceTopSep) {

	function toggleFaderDiv(divID,forceLeftSep,forceTopSep) {
	  	var xOffset = (forceLeftSep==null)?0:forceLeftSep;
		var yOffset = (forceTopSep==null)?0:forceTopSep;
		var scrollPosY = 0;
		var obj = document.getElementById(divID);
		var objCont = getFaderDiv();
		var rX = 0;
		var rY = 0;
		
		if ( obj.style.display == "none"){
			setFaderDivSize();
			
			//Get viewport dimensions
			// the more standards compliant browsers (mozilla/netscape/opera/IE7) use window.innerWidth and window.innerHeight
			if (typeof window.innerWidth != 'undefined') {
			   viewportwidth = window.innerWidth;
			   viewportheight = window.innerHeight;
			 }
			// IE6 in standards compliant mode (i.e. with a valid doctype as the first line in the document)
			else if (typeof document.documentElement != 'undefined' && typeof document.documentElement.clientWidth != 'undefined' && document.documentElement.clientWidth != 0){
				viewportwidth = document.documentElement.clientWidth;
			    viewportheight = document.documentElement.clientHeight;
			 }
			 // older versions of IE
			else{
				viewportwidth = document.getElementsByTagName('body')[0].clientWidth;
			    viewportheight = document.getElementsByTagName('body')[0].clientHeight;
			 }
			
			if(xOffset > 0){
				// Set left to passed poistion
				obj.style.left = xOffset;
			}else{
				// Set horizontal (left) offset to half the width of the layer
				xOffset = (obj.style.width.replace("px","") > 0)? obj.style.width.replace("px","") / 2 : 0 ;	
				// Find the horizontal center of the viewport.
				
				if(document.documentElement && document.documentElement.scrollLeft) {
					rX = document.documentElement.scrollLeft + (viewportwidth/2);
				}else if(document.body) {
					rX = document.body.scrollLeft + (viewportwidth/2);
				}else if(self.pageYOffset) {
					rX = self.pageXOffset + (viewportwidth/2);
				}
				//alert("width" + rX + " : " + xOffset);
				obj.style.left = rX - xOffset ;
			}
			
			if(yOffset > 0){
				// Set top to scroll top + passed position
				if(window.pageYOffset != null){ 
					scrollPosY = window.pageYOffset + yOffset;
				}else if (document.body.scrollTop != null){ 
					scrollPosY = document.body.scrollTop + yOffset;
				}
				obj.style.top = scrollPosY + "px";
			}else{
				// Set vertical (top) offset to half the width of the layer
				yOffset = (obj.style.height.replace("px","") > 0)? obj.style.height.replace("px","") / 2 : 0 ;
				// Find the vertical center of the viewport by height and scroll offset.
				if(document.documentElement && document.documentElement.scrollTop) {
					rY = document.documentElement.scrollTop + (viewportheight/2);
				}else if(document.body) {
					if (document.body.offsetHeight > 0){
						rY = document.body.scrollTop + (viewportheight/2);
					}else{
						rY = document.body.scrollTop + 270;
					}
				}else if(self.pageYOffset) {
					rY = self.pageYOffset + (viewportheight/2);
				}
				//alert("height" + rY + " : " + yOffset);
				obj.style.top = rY - yOffset ;
			}
			
			// Display layers
			//objCont.style.z-index=990;
			objCont.style.display="";
			
			//obj.style.z-index = 999;
			obj.style.display = "";
		}else{
			objCont.style.display="none";
			obj.style.display = "none";
			obj.style.top = 0;
			obj.style.left = 0;
		}
	}
	
	function setFaderDivSize() { // cf_fader div
	// Find Screen size, and x & y scroll ofset we we can precisely size the fader div, or better still, just set dimensions to the entire document size. -GD
		var fdrObj = getFaderDiv();
		var myWidth = 0, myHeight = 0;
		var scrOfX = 0, scrOfY = 0;
			  
		if (document.body.scrollHeight && document.body.scrollWidth ){
	  		// This is the best method, as it covers the entire document, not just the view port (window). GD 
			myWidth = document.body.scrollWidth;
			myHeight = document.body.scrollHeight;
		}else{
			if( typeof( window.innerWidth ) == 'number' ) {
		  		//Non-IE
		  		myWidth = window.innerWidth;
		    	myHeight = window.innerHeight;
			} else if( document.documentElement && ( document.documentElement.clientWidth || document.documentElement.clientHeight ) ) {
		    	//IE 6+ in 'standards compliant mode'
		    	myWidth = document.documentElement.clientWidth;
		    	myHeight = document.documentElement.clientHeight;
			} else if( document.body && ( document.body.clientWidth || document.body.clientHeight ) ) {
		    	//IE 4 compatible
		    	myWidth = document.body.clientWidth;
		    	myHeight = document.body.clientHeight;
			}
		
			if( typeof( window.pageYOffset ) == 'number' ) {
		   		//Netscape compliant
		    	scrOfY = window.pageYOffset;
		    	scrOfX = window.pageXOffset;
		  	} else if( document.body && ( document.body.scrollLeft || document.body.scrollTop ) ) {
		    	//DOM compliant
		    	scrOfY = document.body.scrollTop;
		    	scrOfX = document.body.scrollLeft;
		  	} else if( document.documentElement && ( document.documentElement.scrollLeft || document.documentElement.scrollTop ) ) {
		    	//IE6 standards compliant mode
		    	scrOfY = document.documentElement.scrollTop;
		    	scrOfX = document.documentElement.scrollLeft;
		  	}
			
			myWidth = myWidth + scrOfX;
			myHeight = myHeight + scrOfY + 1000;
		}
		fdrObj.style.height = myHeight ;
		fdrObj.style.width = myWidth ;
	}
	
	</script>

		function loginPopup(overrideReturnURL){ 
			if(overrideReturnURL != null){
				document.forms["CustomerLoginForm"].action = overrideReturnURL;
			}
			toggleFaderDiv('loginFaderContent'); 
		} 

	function nonWhiteSpace(elem,label){
		return GLOBAL_isWhiteSpace(elem.value)?"\n"+ label +" is required.":"";
	}	

	function CheckLogin(thisForm){
		var elems = thisForm.elements;
		errors = ""; 
		
		errors += nonWhiteSpace(elems["homeEmail"],"Email Address");
		errors += nonWhiteSpace(elems["webPassword"],"Password");
		
		if(errors.length){
			alert(errors);
			return false;
		} else{
			return true;
		}
	}
</script>

<script type="text/javascript">
var timeout    = 500;
var closetimer = 0;
var ddmenuitem = 0;

function jsddm_open()
{  jsddm_canceltimer();
   jsddm_close();
   ddmenuitem = $(this).find('ul:has(li)').css('visibility', 'visible');}

function jsddm_close()
{  if(ddmenuitem) ddmenuitem.css('visibility', 'hidden');}

function jsddm_timer()
{  closetimer = window.setTimeout(jsddm_close, timeout);}

function jsddm_canceltimer()
{  if(closetimer)
   {  window.clearTimeout(closetimer);
      closetimer = null;}}

$(document).ready(function()
{  $('#NavList > li').bind('mouseover', jsddm_open);
   $('#NavList > li').bind('mouseout',  jsddm_timer)});

document.onclick = jsddm_close;

</script>

<script language="javascript">
	function showKBBDisclaimer(objID){
		obj = document.getElementById(objID);
		obj.style.display = "";
	}

	function HideKBBDisclaimer(objID){
		obj = document.getElementById(objID);
		obj.style.display = "none";
	}
	
	function toggleAddrDiv(invid){
		var divName = document.getElementById("addrDiv_" + invid).style.display;
		var imgName = document.getElementById("addrImg_" + invid).src;
		document.getElementById("addrDiv_" + invid).style.display = (divName == "none")? "" : "none";
		document.getElementById("addrImg_" + invid).src = (imgName == "http://www.autonation.com/Templates/website/autonation_gamma/images/gamma/+_2.gif")? "/Templates/website/autonation_gamma/images/gamma/__2.gif" : "/Templates/website/autonation_gamma/images/gamma/+_2.gif";
	}

	function expandSelectedRow(expandRowId,highlightRowId,highlightRowOffClass,highlightRowOnClass){
		//alert(expandRowId+ "|" + highlightRowId  + "|" + highlightRowOffClass + "|" +highlightRowOnClass);
		highlightRow = document.getElementById(highlightRowId);
		expandRow = document.getElementById(expandRowId);
		expandItem(expandRowId);
		rowIsExpanded = (expandRow.style.display !== 'none');
		highlightRow.className=rowIsExpanded?highlightRowOnClass:highlightRowOffClass;
	}

	function expandInvItem(theitem,highlightRowId,highlightRowOffClass,highlightRowOnClass){
		opentable = document.getElementById(theitem);
		Tree_ExpanderID = "Tree_Expander_" + theitem;
		Tree_Expander = document.getElementById(Tree_ExpanderID);
		Tree_ExpanderSource = Tree_Expander.src.toLowerCase();
		if(opentable.style.display == "none") {
			if(GetBrowser() == "ie") {
				opentable.style.display = "block";
			} else {
				opentable.style.display = "table-row";
			}
			Tree_Expander.src = Tree_ExpanderSource.replace("expand","collapse");
		}

		highlightRow = document.getElementById(highlightRowId);
		expandRow = document.getElementById(theitem);
		rowIsExpanded = (expandRow.style.display !== 'none');
		highlightRow.className=rowIsExpanded?highlightRowOnClass:highlightRowOffClass;
	}

	function closeInvItem(theitem,highlightRowId,highlightRowOffClass,highlightRowOnClass){
		opentable = document.getElementById(theitem);
		Tree_ExpanderID = "Tree_Expander_" + theitem;
		Tree_Expander = document.getElementById(Tree_ExpanderID);
		Tree_ExpanderSource = Tree_Expander.src.toLowerCase();

		opentable.style.display = "none";
		Tree_Expander.src = Tree_ExpanderSource.replace("collapse","expand");

		highlightRow = document.getElementById(highlightRowId);
		expandRow = document.getElementById(theitem);
		rowIsExpanded = (expandRow.style.display !== 'none');
		highlightRow.className=rowIsExpanded?highlightRowOnClass:highlightRowOffClass;
	}

	function isValidEmail(anEmail){
			regEmail = /^[A-Za-z0-9\-_]+(\.[A-Za-z0-9\-_]+)*@([A-Za-z0-9\-_\.]+\.)+[A-Za-z]{2,3}$/i;
			return regEmail.test(anEmail);
	}

	function findPosX(obj)	{
		var curleft = 0;
		if (obj.offsetParent)
		{
			while (obj.offsetParent)
			{
				curleft += obj.offsetLeft
				obj = obj.offsetParent;
			}
		}
		else if (obj.x)
			curleft += obj.x;
		return curleft;
	}

	function findPosY(obj)
	{
		var curtop = 0;
		if (obj.offsetParent)
		{
			while (obj.offsetParent)
			{
				curtop += obj.offsetTop
				obj = obj.offsetParent;
			}
		}
		else if (obj.y)
			curtop += obj.y;

		return curtop;
	}

	function toggleLayer(objID,posId,type)
	{
		if(type == "new"){
			var filterlist ="msrp,vehicle";
		}
		else {
			var filterlist ="price,vehicle";
		}

		var selectlist ="a,b";
		var ArrSelect = selectlist.split(",");
		var ArrFilter = filterlist.split(",");
		var mystyleid = posId+'td';


		//close all other filter selection except for the one clicked
		var myfilter = "";
		   for(i=0;i < ArrFilter.length;i++){
		    	myfilter = ArrFilter[i];
		    	myselect  = ArrSelect[i]+'td';
		   		if( objID != myfilter && document.getElementById( myfilter ) ){

					document.getElementById(myfilter).style.display = "none";
					document.getElementById(myfilter).style.top = 0;
					document.getElementById(myfilter).style.left = 0;
					//document.getElementById(myselect).style.backgroundColor = "#ff6600";

		   		}
		  	}

		if (document.getElementById)
		{
			// this is the way the standards work
			var obj = document.getElementById(objID);
			var pos = document.getElementById(posId);

			if ( obj.style.display == "none")
			{
				//document.getElementById(mystyleid).style.backgroundColor = "#003366";
				obj.style.top = findPosY(pos)+ 20;
				obj.style.left = findPosX(pos)-2;
				obj.style.display = "";

			}
			else
			{
				//document.getElementById(mystyleid).style.backgroundColor = "#003366";
				obj.style.display = "none";
				obj.style.top = 0;
				obj.style.left = 0;
			}
		}

	}

	
	
	/* 	JavaScript used to minimize effects of the overLink div. When a customer mouses over
		the Window Sticker link, linkClear is set to false. This eliminates a problem with the
		overLink onclick event being fired at the same time as the Window Sticker link. */

	var linkClear = true;

	function goOverLink(url)
	{
		if (linkClear == true)
		{
			document.location.href = url;
		}
	}
	function disableOverLink()
	{
		linkClear = false;
	}
	function enableOverLink()
	{
		linkClear = true;
	}
</script>

	// These objects store the checkbox indexes for models by make and trims by model
	var modelIdxs = new Object();
	var modelsChecked = new Array();
	function buildModelIdxs(){
		var thisMake = "";
		var lastMake = "";
		for(i=0;i<modelElems.length;i++){
			splitString = modelElems[i].split('|');
			thisMake = splitString[0];
			if(thisMake != lastMake){
				modelIdxs[thisMake] = new Array();
				modelIdxs[thisMake].push(i); 
			}else{
				modelIdxs[thisMake].push(i);
			}
			lastMake = thisMake
		}
	}
	buildModelIdxs()

	var trimIdxs = new Object();
	var trimsChecked = new Array();
	function buildTrimIdxs(){
		var thisModel = "";
		var lastModel = "";
		for(i=0;i<trimElems.length;i++){
			splitString = trimElems[i].split('|');
			thisModel = splitString[1];
			if(thisModel != lastModel){
				trimIdxs[thisModel] = new Array();
				trimIdxs[thisModel].push(i); 
			}else{
				trimIdxs[thisModel].push(i);
			}
			lastModel = thisModel
		}
	}
	buildTrimIdxs();
	
	function toggleFilterDisplay(filterName){	
		var divName = document.getElementById("searchfilter_" + filterName).style.display;
		if(activeMultiFldName.length > 0){
			alert("Please Update or Cancel active multiple select before proceeding");
		}else{
			if(divName == "none"){
				document.getElementById("searchfilter_" + filterName).style.display = "";
				document.getElementById("button_" + filterName).style.background = "url(/Templates/website/autonation_gamma/images/gamma/search_box_bk.gif)";
				document.getElementById(filterName + "IMG").src = "/Templates/website/autonation_gamma/images/gamma/_.gif";	
			}else{
				document.getElementById("searchfilter_" + filterName).style.display = "none";
				document.getElementById("button_" + filterName).style.background = "";
				document.getElementById(filterName + "IMG").src = "/Templates/website/autonation_gamma/images/gamma/+.gif";
			}
		}
	}
	
	function toggleMultiSelect(fldName,action){
		var toRestore = "";
		var thisFldName = "";
		var isMatch = false;
		var thisMultiValIndxLen = "";
		
		if(action == 'on' && activeMultiFldName.length > 0){
			alert("Please Update or Cancel active multiple select before proceeding");
		}else{
			activeMultiFldName = (action == "on")?fldName:"";
			if(action == 'on'){
				//disable all fields except the active multiselect
				for(i=0;i<document.searchfilter.elements.length;i++){
					thisFldName = fldName.split(",");
					for(j=0;j<thisFldName.length;j++){
						if(thisFldName[j] == document.searchfilter.elements[i].name){
							isMatch = true;
						}	
					}
					if(isMatch == false){
						document.searchfilter.elements[i].disabled = true;		
					}
				}
				//toggle button display
				if(fldName == "trans,engine,drivetype"){
					document.getElementById("mslinkoff_drivetrain").style.display = "none";
					document.getElementById("mslinkon_drivetrain").style.display = "";
					document.getElementById("mslinkupd_drivetrain").style.display = "";
					document.getElementById("mslinkupd2_drivetrain").style.display = "";		
				}else{
					document.getElementById("mslinkoff_" + fldName).style.display = "none";
					document.getElementById("mslinkon_" + fldName).style.display = "";
					document.getElementById("mslinkupd_" + fldName).style.display = "";
					document.getElementById("mslinkupd2_" + fldName).style.display = "";
				}
			}else{
				//re-enable form fields
				for(i=0;i<document.searchfilter.elements.length;i++){
					document.searchfilter.elements[i].disabled = false;
				}
				//toggle button display
				if(fldName == "trans,engine,drivetype"){
					document.getElementById("mslinkoff_drivetrain").style.display = "";
					document.getElementById("mslinkon_drivetrain").style.display = "none";
					document.getElementById("mslinkupd_drivetrain").style.display = "none";
					document.getElementById("mslinkupd2_drivetrain").style.display = "none";	
				}else{
					document.getElementById("mslinkoff_" + fldName).style.display = "";
					document.getElementById("mslinkon_" + fldName).style.display = "none";
					document.getElementById("mslinkupd_" + fldName).style.display = "none";
					document.getElementById("mslinkupd2_" + fldName).style.display = "none";
				}
			}
			//restore stored multiple form selections to original values and remove array elements
			thisMultiValIndxLen = activeMultiValIndx.length
			for (i=thisMultiValIndxLen-1;i>=0;i--){
				toRestore = activeMultiValIndx[i].split(",");
				if(toRestore.length > 0){
					//alert(toRestore[0] + "-" + toRestore[1]);
					document.searchfilter[toRestore[0]][toRestore[1]].checked = (toRestore[2] == "on")? false : true ;
				}
				activeMultiValIndx.pop();
			}
		}
	}
	
	function clearSearchFilter(fldname,fldval,subform,fldParent,fldGrandParent){
		if(fldname == "PriceRange"){
			document.searchfilter["StartPriceRange"].value = "";
			document.searchfilter["EndPriceRange"].value = "";
		}else if(fldname == "YearRange"){
			document.searchfilter["StartYearRange"].value = "";
			document.searchfilter["EndYearRange"].value = "";
		}else if(fldname == "mpg"){
			document.searchfilter["mpg"][0].checked = true;
		}else{
			for(i=0;i<document.searchfilter.elements.length;i++){
				//alert(document.searchfilter.elements[i].type + " : " + document.searchfilter.elements[i].name + " = " + document.searchfilter.elements[i].value);
				if(document.searchfilter.elements[i].name == fldname && document.searchfilter.elements[i].value == fldval){
					if(document.searchfilter.elements[i].type == "checkbox"){
						document.searchfilter.elements[i].checked = false;
					}else if(document.searchfilter.elements[i].type == "radio"){
						document.searchfilter.elements[i].checked = false;
					}else if(document.searchfilter.elements[i].type == "select"){
						document.searchfilter.elements[i].options.length = 0;
					}else if(document.searchfilter.elements[i].type != "radio"){
						document.searchfilter.elements[i].value = "";	
					}
				}
			}
		}
		if(fldname == "make" || fldname == "model" || fldname == "trim"){	
			chkMakeModelTrim(fldname,fldval,fldParent,fldGrandParent,false);
		}			
		if(subform){
			submitSearchFilters('','');
		}
	}
	
	function clearAllSearchFilters(subform){
		if(subform){
			window.location.href="index.cfm?action=inventorysearch&subaction=searchlist_gamma&zipcode=77423&sendinfo=Submit&inventorytype=used";
		}else{
			for(i=0;i<document.searchfilter.elements.length;i++){
				if(document.searchfilter.elements[i].type == "checkbox"){
					document.searchfilter.elements[i].checked = false;
				}else if(document.searchfilter.elements[i].type == "radio"){
					document.searchfilter.elements[i].checked = false;
				}else if(document.searchfilter.elements[i].type == "select"){
					document.searchfilter.elements[i].options.length = 0;
				}else if(document.searchfilter.elements[i].type != "radio"){
					document.searchfilter.elements[i].value = "";	
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	function enableFormFields(){
		for(i=0;i<document.searchfilter.elements.length;i++){
			document.searchfilter.elements[i].disabled = false;
		}
	}
	
	function toggleChecked(fld){
		var frmFld = document.searchfilter[fld.name];
		if(fld.value == ""){
			for(i=1;i<frmFld.length;i++){
				frmFld[i].checked = false;
			}
		}else{
			frmFld[0].checked = false;
		}
	}
	
	function checkboxRadio(fld){
		var frmFld = document.searchfilter[fld.name];
		if(frmFld.length){
			for(i=0;i<frmFld.length;i++){
				if(frmFld[i].value != fld.value){	
					frmFld[i].checked = false;
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	function chkMakeModelTrim(fldName,fldValue,fldParent,fldGrandParent,fldChecked){
		if(fldName == "make" && modelElems.length > 0){	
			if(! fldChecked){
				//Remove any children of this make
				//alert(modelIdxs[fld.value].length + " : " + document.searchfilter.model.length + " : " + modelElems.length);
				//alert(modelElems);
				for(i=0;i<modelIdxs[fldValue].length;i++){
					thisModelIdx =  modelIdxs[fldValue][i];
					thisModel = document.searchfilter.model[thisModelIdx].value;
					if(document.searchfilter.model[thisModelIdx].checked){
						document.searchfilter.model[thisModelIdx].checked = false ;
						for(j=0;j<trimIdxs[thisModel].length;j++){
							thisTrimIdx = trimIdxs[thisModel][j];
							document.searchfilter.trim[thisTrimIdx].checked = false;
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}else if(fldName == "model"){
			if(! fldChecked && trimElems.length > 0){ 	
				//Remove any children of this model
				if(trimIdxs[fldValue].length > 1){
					for(i=0;i<trimIdxs[fldValue].length;i++){
						thisTrimIdx = trimIdxs[fldValue][i];
						document.searchfilter.trim[thisTrimIdx].checked = false;
					}
				}else if(trimIdxs[fldValue].length = 1){
					document.searchfilter.trim.checked = false
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	function procInventoryTypeChange(newtype){
		if(newtype == "new" || newtype == "New"){
			clearSearchFilter('YearRange',false);
			clearSearchFilter('mileage',false);
			
		}
		submitSearchFilters('inventorytype',newtype);
	}
	
	function procYearSubmit(){
		if(document.searchfilter["StartYearRange"].value == ""){
			document.searchfilter["StartYearRange"].value = 1995;
		}
		if(document.searchfilter["EndYearRange"].value == ""){
			document.searchfilter["EndYearRange"].value = 2013;
		}
		submitSearchFilters('yr','0');		
	}
	
	function gaTrackLink(fldName,fldVal){
		var gaAction = "";
		var gaLabel = "";
		var thisMultiValIdx = "";
		var multiValStr = "";
		
		//This routine creates a pipe delimited list of multiple selections
		if(activeMultiValIndx.length > 0){
			for (i=0;i<activeMultiValIndx.length;i++){
				thisMultiValIdx = activeMultiValIndx[i].split(",");
				if(thisMultiValIdx[2] == "on"){
					if(multiValStr.length > 0 ){
						multiValStr += "|";
					}
					multiValStr += document.searchfilter[thisMultiValIdx[0]][thisMultiValIdx[1]].value
					if(thisMultiValIdx[0]=="engine"){
						multiValStr += " Cyl";
					} 
				}
			}
			fldVal = multiValStr;
		}else if(fldVal == ""){// "All" values are expressed in the form fields as empty strings
			fldVal="All";
		}
		
		//alert("h1");
		if(fldVal.length > 0){
			switch(fldName){
				case 'inventorytype':
					gaAction = fldVal + '_Search Filter';
					gaLabel = 'Left Nav_New or Used';
					break;
				case 'price':
					gaAction = 'Price_Search Filter';
					if(isNaN(document.searchfilter["StartPriceRange"].value)){document.searchfilter["StartPriceRange"].value = 0;}
					if(isNaN(document.searchfilter["EndPriceRange"].value)){document.searchfilter["EndPriceRange"].value = 0;}
					gaLabel = 'Left Nav_Price_' + document.searchfilter["StartPriceRange"].value + ':' + document.searchfilter["EndPriceRange"].value;
					break;
				case 'EndYearRange':
					gaAction = 'Year_Search Filter';
					if(isNaN(document.searchfilter["StartYearRange"].value)){document.searchfilter["StartYearRange"].value = document.searchfilter["EndYearRange"].value;}
					if(isNaN(document.searchfilter["EndYearRange"].value)){document.searchfilter["EndYearRange"].value = document.searchfilter["StartYearRange"].value;}
					if(document.searchfilter["StartYearRange"].value == document.searchfilter["EndYearRange"].value){
						gaLabel = 'Left Nav_Year_' + document.searchfilter["StartYearRange"].value;
					}else{
						gaLabel = 'Left Nav_Year_' + document.searchfilter["StartYearRange"].value + ':' + document.searchfilter["EndYearRange"].value;
					}
					break;
				case 'make':
					gaAction = 'Make_Search Filter';
					gaLabel = 'Left Nav_Make_' + fldVal;
					break;
				case 'model':
					gaAction = 'Model_Search Filter';
					gaLabel = 'Left Nav_Model_' + fldVal;
					break;
				case 'trim':
					gaAction = 'Trim_Search Filter';
					gaLabel = 'Left Nav_Trim_' + fldVal;
					break;
				case 'bodycategory':
					gaAction = fldVal + '_Search Filter';
					gaLabel = 'Left Nav_Body Type';
					break;
				case 'trans,engine,drivetype':
					gaAction = fldVal + '_Search Filter';
					gaLabel = 'Left Nav_Engine/Trans/DriveType';
					break;
				case 'trans':
					gaAction = fldVal + '_Search Filter';
					gaLabel = 'Left Nav_Engine/Trans/DriveType';
					break;
				case 'engine':
					gaAction = fldVal + ' Cyl_Search Filter';
					gaLabel = 'Left Nav_Engine/Trans/DriveType';
					break;
				case 'drivetype':
					gaAction = fldVal + '_Search Filter';
					gaLabel = 'Left Nav_Engine/Trans/DriveType';
					break;
				case 'CarFaxICRAvailable':
					gaAction = 'CarFax Available_Search Filter';
					gaLabel = 'Left Nav_CarFax';
					break;
				case 'CarfaxOneOwnerVehicle':
					gaAction = 'CarFax 1 Owner_Search Filter';
					gaLabel = 'Left Nav_CarFax';
					break;
				case 'availability':
					if(fldVal == "FTB"){
						gaAction = 'Available for Transfer_Search Filter';
					}else if(fldVal == "T"){
						gaAction = 'In Transit_Search Filter';
					}else{
						gaAction = 'In Stock_Search Filter';
					}
					gaLabel = 'Left Nav_Availability';
					break;
					
				default:
					gaAction = fldVal + '_Search Filter';
					gaLabel = 'Left Nav_' + fldName;
			}
					
			//alert(gaAction + " : " + gaLabel);
			
			pageTracker._trackEvent('Search Results Page', gaAction, gaLabel);
			globalTracker._trackEvent('Search Results Page', gaAction, gaLabel);
		}
	}
		
	function procFilterClick(fld,fldMode,fldIdx,fldParent,fldGrandParent){
		var isMulti = false;
		var msswitch = "";
		var multiFldNames = activeMultiFldName.split(",");
		var subform = true;
		var thisMake = "";
		var thisModel = "";
		var thisTrim = "";
		for(i=0;i<multiFldNames.length;i++){
			if(multiFldNames[i] == fld.name){isMulti = true;}
		}
		if(activeMultiFldName.length == 0 || isMulti){	
			if(isMulti){
				msswitch = (fld.checked)? "on":"off";
				activeMultiValIndx.push(fld.name + "," + fldIdx + "," + msswitch);
				subform = false;
			}else if(fldMode == "singlecheck"){
				checkboxRadio(fld);
			}
		}else{
			alert("Please update or cancel your multiple selections before proceeding.");
			subform = false;
		}
		if(fld.name == "make" || fld.name == "model" || fld.name == "trim"){	
			chkMakeModelTrim(fld.name,fld.value,fldParent,fldGrandParent,fld.checked);
		}
		if(subform){
			submitSearchFilters(fld.name,fld.value);
		}
	}
	
	function submitSearchFilters(fldName,fldVal){
		if(!formSubbed){
			var theURL="index.cfm?action=inventorysearch&subaction=searchlist_gamma&zipcode=77423&sendinfo=Submit";
			var lastelem = "";
			for( i=0;i<document.searchfilter.elements.length;i++){
				elem=document.searchfilter.elements[i];
				if(elem.name!=""){
					if(((elem.type=="text" || elem.type=="hidden") ||((elem.type=="radio" || elem.type=="checkbox") && elem.checked)) && elem.value != "" && elem.value != 0 ){
						if(elem.name == lastelem){	
							theURL += "," + elem.value;
						}else{	
							theURL += "&" + elem.name + "=" + elem.value;
						}
						lastelem = elem.name;
					}
				}
			}
			
			if(fldName.length > 0){
				gaTrackLink(fldName,fldVal);
			}
			
			formSubbed = true;
			//alert("FIN!");
			centerLoadImg();
			toggleFaderDiv('procImgFrame');
			window.location.href=theURL;
			
			
				imgDiv = document.getElementById("procImgFrame");
				imgNode=imgDiv.getElementsByTagName("img")[0];
				imgNode.src=imgNode.src;		//complete hack for IE which tricks the animated gif into animating while page loads.
			
		}
	}
	
	function centerLoadImg() {
	  	var rX,rY
		if(document.documentElement && document.documentElement.scrollTop) {
			rX = document.documentElement.scrollLeft + ((document.documentElement.clientWidth/2)-150);
			rY = document.documentElement.scrollTop + ((document.documentElement.clientHeight/2)-30);
		}else if(document.body) {
			rX = document.body.scrollLeft + ((document.body.offsetWidth/2)-150);
			if (document.body.offsetHeight > 0){
				rY = document.body.scrollTop + ((document.body.offsetHeight/2)-30);
			}else{
				rY = document.body.scrollTop + 270;
			}
		}else if(self.pageYOffset) {
			rX = self.pageXOffset + ((window.innerWidth/2)-150);
			rY = self.pageYOffset + ((window.innerHeight/2)-30);
		}
		document.getElementById("procImgFrame").style.left = rX;
		document.getElementById("procImgFrame").style.top = rY;
		window.setTimeout("centerLoadImg()", 10);
	}

			document.getElementById("faderDiv").style.display = "";

			setFaderDivSize(5000);
		}else{

		}

			<div id="button_year" class="AccordionHead" onClick="toggleFilterDisplay('year')">
		        <span><img id="yearIMG" src="/Templates/website/autonation_gamma/images/gamma/+.gif" width="9" height="9" align="expand" border="0" /></span>
		        <span class="AccordionTitle">YEAR</span>
		    </div>
			<div id="searchfilter_year" class="filterItemField" style="display:none;text-align:left;">
				
					<script language="JavaScript" type="text/javascript">
						//var yrArray = new Array("Any",1995,1997,1998,1999,2000,2001,2002,2003,2004,2005,2006,2007,2008,2009,2010,2011,2012,2013);
						var yrArray = new Array(1995,1997,1998,1999,2000,2001,2002,2003,2004,2005,2006,2007,2008,2009,2010,2011,2012,2013);
						
						function updateEndYear(fld){
							var thisFldVal = fld.value;
							var updFld = document.searchfilter["EndYearRangeSel"];
							var endYrSelectedVal = updFld.options[updFld.length -1].value;
							if(updFld.selectedIndex > -1){
								endYrSelectedVal = 	updFld.options[updFld.selectedIndex].value;	
							}
							updFld.options.length=0;
							for(i=0;i<yrArray.length;i++){
								//if(yrArray[i] == "Any" || yrArray[i] > thisFldVal ){
								if(yrArray[i] >= thisFldVal ){
									updFld[updFld.options.length]=new Option(yrArray[i],yrArray[i],false,(yrArray[i] == endYrSelectedVal));
								}	
							}
							document.searchfilter["StartYearRange"].value = thisFldVal;
							if(document.searchfilter["EndYearRange"].value == ""){
								document.searchfilter["EndYearRange"].value = 2013;
							}		
						}
						
						function updateStartYear(fld){
							var thisFldVal = fld.value;
							var updFld = document.searchfilter["StartYearRangeSel"];
							var endYrSelectedVal = updFld.options[updFld.length -1].value;
							if(updFld.selectedIndex > -1){
								endYrSelectedVal = 	updFld.options[updFld.selectedIndex].value;	
							}
							updFld.options.length=0;
							for(i=0;i<yrArray.length;i++){
								//if(yrArray[i] == "Any" || yrArray[i] < thisFldVal){
								if(yrArray[i] <= thisFldVal){
									updFld[updFld.options.length]=new Option(yrArray[i],yrArray[i],false,(yrArray[i] == endYrSelectedVal));
								}	
							}
							document.searchfilter["EndYearRange"].value = thisFldVal;
							if(document.searchfilter["StartYearRange"].value == ""){
								document.searchfilter["StartYearRange"].value = 1995;
							}	
									
						}
					</script>

	<script language="javascript">
		function isValidEmail(anEmail){
			regEmail = /^[A-Za-z0-9\-_]+(\.[A-Za-z0-9\-_]+)*@([A-Za-z0-9\-_\.]+\.)+[A-Za-z]{2,3}$/i;
			return regEmail.test(anEmail);
		}
		function isValidZipCode(zipCode){
			zipPattern = /(^\d{5}$)/ ;
			return zipPattern.test(zipCode);
		}
		function validateQuickContact(thisForm){
			errors = "";
			errors += (thisForm.elements.firstname.value.length < 2)?"\nFirst Name is required.":"";
			errors += (thisForm.elements.lastname.value.length < 2)?"\nLast Name is required.":"";
			errors += (!isValidEmail(thisForm.elements.homeemail.value))?"\nA valid email address is required.":"";
			isValidAreaCode = ((!isNaN(thisForm.elements.homephonearea.value)) && thisForm.elements.homephonearea.value.length == 3);
			isValidPhonePrefix = ((!isNaN(thisForm.elements.homephoneprefix.value)) && thisForm.elements.homephoneprefix.value.length == 3) ;
			isValidPhoneSuffix = ((!isNaN(thisForm.elements.homephonesuffix.value)) && thisForm.elements.homephonesuffix.value.length == 4);
			errors += (!isValidAreaCode || !isValidPhonePrefix || !isValidPhoneSuffix)?"\nA valid phone number is required.":"";
			//errors += (thisForm.elements.customerZipCode.value.length == 0)?"\nZip Code is required.":"";
			errors += (!isValidZipCode(thisForm.elements.customerZipCode.value))?"\nA valid zip code is required.":"";
			
			errors += (thisForm.elements.yr.options[thisForm.elements.yr.selectedIndex].value.length == 0)?"\nVehicle Year is required.":"";
			errors += (thisForm.elements.make.options[thisForm.elements.make.selectedIndex].value.length == 0)?"\nVehicle Make is required.":"";
			errors += (thisForm.elements.model.options[thisForm.elements.model.selectedIndex].value.length == 0)?"\nVehicle Model is required.":"";
			
			if(errors.length){
				alert(errors);
				//return false;
			} else{
				document.quickContact.submit();
				//return true;
			}
		}

	function limitText(limitField, limitCount, limitNum, counterId) {
		var bName = navigator.appName;			
		if (limitField.value.length > limitNum) {
			limitField.value = limitField.value.substring(0, limitNum);
		} else {
			limitCount.value = limitNum - limitField.value.length;
		if(bName == "Netscape"){	
			document.getElementById(counterId).textContent=limitNum - limitField.value.length + " Characters Remaining";
			}
		else{			
			document.getElementById(counterId).innerText=limitNum - limitField.value.length + " Characters Remaining";
			}
		}
	}		
		
	</script>

<script language="javascript">
	// functions to return constants
	var vehicleSelectorForm2008517817353 = document.forms["quickContact"];

	function getCertifiedCheckbox2008517817353(){
		return vehicleSelectorForm2008517817353.elements["certified"];	
	}
	function getYearSelector2008517817353(){
		return vehicleSelectorForm2008517817353.elements["yr"];
	}
	function getMakeSelector2008517817353(){
		return vehicleSelectorForm2008517817353.elements["make"];
	}
	function getModelSelector2008517817353(){
		return vehicleSelectorForm2008517817353.elements["model"];
	}
	function getScriptsURL2008517817353(){
		var scriptsURL = document.location.protocol + "//www.autonation.com/com/autofuse/inventory";
		return scriptsURL;
	}
	function getVehicleType2008517817353(){
		var vehicleType = "New"
		
		return vehicleType;
	}
	
	function getRequestingFranchiseId2008517817353(){
		return "2822";
	}
	function getRadioValue2008517817353(aRadio){
		radioValue = "";
		if(aRadio.length > 0){
			for(i=0; i<aRadio.length; i++){
				radioValue = (aRadio[i].checked)?aRadio[i].value:radioValue;
			}
		} else{
			radioValue = (aRadio.checked)?aRadio.value:radioValue;
		}
		return radioValue;
	}
	function newXMLHttpRequest2008517817353() {
		var xmlreq = false;
		if (window.XMLHttpRequest) {
			xmlreq = new XMLHttpRequest();
		} else if (window.ActiveXObject) {
			try {
				xmlreq = new ActiveXObject("Microsoft.XMLHTTP");
			}
			catch (e2) {
				alert("Unable to create a Microsoft.XMLHTTP XMLHttpRequest.");
			}
		}
		return xmlreq;
	}
	function getYearSelectedValue2008517817353(){
		return "";
	}
	function getShowYearSelectorForNewCars2008517817353(){
		return ("1" == "1")?true:false;
	}
	function getShowYearSelectorForUsedCars2008517817353(){
		return ("0" == "1")?true:false;
	}
	function getMakeSelectedValue2008517817353(){
		return "Corporate";
	}
	function getModelSelectedValue2008517817353(){
		return "";
	}

	/*
	 * Returns a function that waits for the specified XMLHttpRequest to complete, then passes its XML response to the given handler function.
	 * req - The XMLHttpRequest whose state is changing
	 * responseXmlHandler - Function to pass the XML response to
	 */
	function getReadyStateHandler2008517817353(req, responseXmlHandler) {
	  // If the request's status is "complete" (4) , then Check that a "successful" (200)server response was received
	  // and pass the XML payload of the response to the handler function
	  //alert("in handler - request.readystate was: " + req.status);
	  return function () { if (req.readyState == 4) { (req.status == 200)?responseXmlHandler(req.responseXML):""; } }
	}
	function clearSelect(selectObject){
		while (selectObject.options.length) selectObject.options[0] = null;
		return true;
	}
	function disableSelector(aSelector){
		aSelector.disabled = true;
		aSelector.options[0].text = "Loading...";
		return;
	}
	function enableSelector(aSelector){
		aSelector.disabled = false;
		return;
	}

	function fetchAvailableYears2008517817353(requestingFranchiseId,vehicleType){
		if(	getShowYearSelectorForNewCars2008517817353() && (getVehicleType2008517817353() == "New") ){
			document.getElementById("yearSelectorTR2008517817353").style.display="";	
		}else if (getShowYearSelectorForUsedCars2008517817353() && (getVehicleType2008517817353() == "Used") ){
			document.getElementById("yearSelectorTR2008517817353").style.display="";	
		}else{
			document.getElementById("yearSelectorTR2008517817353").style.display="none";		
		}
			
		disableSelector(getYearSelector2008517817353());
		var fetchAvailableYears2008517817353Request = newXMLHttpRequest2008517817353();
		// Set the handler function to receive callback notifications from the request object
		var handlerFunction = getReadyStateHandler2008517817353(fetchAvailableYears2008517817353Request, populateYearSelector2008517817353);
		var fetchAvailableYears2008517817353URL = getScriptsURL2008517817353() + "/getinstockyearsxml.cfm?&zipCode=&radius=&rooftopId=&city=&state=&requestingFranchiseID=" + requestingFranchiseId + "&vehicleType=" + vehicleType;
		fetchAvailableYears2008517817353Request.onreadystatechange = handlerFunction;
		fetchAvailableYears2008517817353Request.open("POST", fetchAvailableYears2008517817353URL, true);		// Open an HTTP POST connection. Third parameter specifies request is asynchronous.
		fetchAvailableYears2008517817353Request.setRequestHeader("Content-Type", "application/x-www-form-urlencoded");		// Specify that the body of the request contains form data
		fetchAvailableYears2008517817353Request.send("");
	}

	function populateYearSelector2008517817353(responseXML) {
		yearSelector = getYearSelector2008517817353();
		//clear whatever options may already be in there
		clearSelect(yearSelector);
		yearSelector.options[0] = new Option("Select a Year*","",false,false);
		// populate the selector
		var selected = false;
		var years = responseXML.getElementsByTagName("year");
		for (var i = 0 ; i < years.length ; i++) {
			if(years[i].firstChild !== null){
				year = years[i].firstChild.nodeValue;
				if (year == getYearSelectedValue2008517817353()) {
					selected = true;
				} else {
					selected = false;
				}
				yearSelector.options[yearSelector.options.length] = new Option(year,year,false,selected);
			}
		}
		//only "re-enable" the year selector if the user wants the year selector enabled for new vehicles
		if(getShowYearSelectorForNewCars2008517817353() && (getVehicleType2008517817353() == "New")){
			// its a new vehicle and the user doesn't want to show year selector for new vehicles
			enableSelector(yearSelector);
		} 
		else if(getShowYearSelectorForUsedCars2008517817353() && (getVehicleType2008517817353() == "Used")){
			enableSelector(yearSelector);
		} 
		else{
			yearSelector.options[0].text = "All New Vehicle Years";
		}

	}

		fetchAvailableMakes2008517817353Request.onreadystatechange = handlerFunction;

		fetchAvailableMakes2008517817353Request.setRequestHeader("Content-Type", "application/x-www-form-urlencoded");		// Specify that the body of the request contains form data
		fetchAvailableMakes2008517817353Request.send("");
	}

		fetchAvailableMakes2008517817353Request.setRequestHeader("Content-Type", "application/x-www-form-urlencoded");		// Specify that the body of the request contains form data
		fetchAvailableMakes2008517817353Request.send("");
	}
	function populateMakeSelector2008517817353(responseXML) {
		makeSelector = getMakeSelector2008517817353();
		selectedMake = '' ;
		//get the make thats currently selected
		//selectedMake = makeSelector.options[makeSelector.selectedIndex].value;
		//clear whatever options may already be in there
		clearSelect(makeSelector);
		makeSelector.options[0] = new Option("Select a Make*","",false,false);
		var selected = false;
		var makes = responseXML.getElementsByTagName("make");
		for (var i = 0 ; i < makes.length ; i++) {
			if(makes[i].firstChild !== null){
				make = makes[i].firstChild.nodeValue;
				if ((getVehicleType2008517817353().toLowerCase() == "new" || getVehicleType2008517817353().toLowerCase() == "cpo") && make == getMakeSelectedValue2008517817353()) {
					selected = true;
				} else {
					selected = false;
				}
				makeSelector.options[makeSelector.options.length] = new Option(make,make,false,selected);
			}
		}
		enableSelector(makeSelector);
	}
	function fetchAvailableModels2008517817353(requestingFranchiseId,vehicleType,make,yr){
		disableSelector(getModelSelector2008517817353());
		var fetchAvailableModels2008517817353Request = newXMLHttpRequest2008517817353();
		// Set the handler function to receive callback notifications from the request object
		var handlerFunction = getReadyStateHandler2008517817353(fetchAvailableModels2008517817353Request, populateModelSelector2008517817353);
		var fetchAvailableModels2008517817353URL = getScriptsURL2008517817353() + "/getinstockmodelsxml.cfm?&zipCode=&radius=&rooftopId=&city=&state=&requestingFranchiseID=" + requestingFranchiseId + "&vehicleType=" + vehicleType + "&yr=" + yr + "&make=" + make;
		//document.write(fetchAvailableModels2008517817353URL);
		fetchAvailableModels2008517817353Request.onreadystatechange = handlerFunction;
		fetchAvailableModels2008517817353Request.open("POST", fetchAvailableModels2008517817353URL, true);		// Open an HTTP POST connection. Third parameter specifies request is asynchronous.
		fetchAvailableModels2008517817353Request.setRequestHeader("Content-Type", "application/x-www-form-urlencoded");		// Specify that the body of the request contains form data
		fetchAvailableModels2008517817353Request.send("");
	}
	function fetchAvailableCertifiedModels2008517817353(requestingFranchiseId,vehicleType,make,certified){
		disableSelector(getModelSelector2008517817353());
		var fetchAvailableModels2008517817353Request = newXMLHttpRequest2008517817353();
		// Set the handler function to receive callback notifications from the request object
		var handlerFunction = getReadyStateHandler2008517817353(fetchAvailableModels2008517817353Request, populateModelSelector2008517817353);
		var fetchAvailableModels2008517817353URL = getScriptsURL2008517817353() + "/getinstockmodelsxml.cfm?&zipCode=&radius=&rooftopId=&city=&state=&requestingFranchiseID=" + requestingFranchiseId + "&vehicleType=" + vehicleType + "&make=" + make + "&certified=" + certified;
		//document.write(fetchAvailableModels2008517817353URL);
		fetchAvailableModels2008517817353Request.onreadystatechange = handlerFunction;
		fetchAvailableModels2008517817353Request.open("POST", fetchAvailableModels2008517817353URL, true);		// Open an HTTP POST connection. Third parameter specifies request is asynchronous.
		fetchAvailableModels2008517817353Request.setRequestHeader("Content-Type", "application/x-www-form-urlencoded");		// Specify that the body of the request contains form data
		fetchAvailableModels2008517817353Request.send("");
	}

	function populateModelSelector2008517817353(responseXML) {
		modelSelector = getModelSelector2008517817353();
		//clear whatever options may already be in there
		clearSelect(modelSelector);
		modelSelector.options[0] = new Option("Select a Model*","",false,false);
		var selected = false;
		var models = responseXML.getElementsByTagName("model");
		for (var i = 0 ; i < models.length ; i++) {
			if(models[i].firstChild !== null){
				model = models[i].firstChild.nodeValue;
				if (model == getModelSelectedValue2008517817353()) {
					selected = true;
				} else {
					selected = false;
				}
				modelSelector.options[modelSelector.options.length] = new Option(model,model.replace("&","%26"),false,selected);
			}
		}
		enableSelector(modelSelector);
	}

	function changeYearEvent2008517817353(yearSelector){
		thisForm = yearSelector.form;
		selectedYear = yearSelector.options[yearSelector.selectedIndex].value;
		selectedVehicleType = getVehicleType2008517817353();
		requestingFranchiseId = getRequestingFranchiseId2008517817353();
		fetchAvailableMakes2008517817353(requestingFranchiseId,selectedVehicleType,selectedYear);
		//selectedMake = thisForm.make.options[thisForm.make.selectedIndex].value;
		//selectedMake = '';
		//fetchAvailableModels2008517817353(requestingFranchiseId,selectedVehicleType,selectedYear,selectedMake);
		//selectedModel = '';
	}
	function changeMakeEvent2008517817353(makeSelector){
		thisForm = makeSelector.form;
		yearSelector = getYearSelector2008517817353();
		selectedYear = yearSelector.options[yearSelector.selectedIndex].value;
		selectedMake = makeSelector.options[makeSelector.selectedIndex].value;
		selectedVehicleType = getVehicleType2008517817353();
		requestingFranchiseId = getRequestingFranchiseId2008517817353();
		
		
			fetchAvailableModels2008517817353(requestingFranchiseId,selectedVehicleType,selectedMake,selectedYear);
		
		
		//fetchAvailableModels2008517817353(requestingFranchiseId,selectedVehicleType,selectedMake);
		
	}
	
	function buildMenus2008517817353(){
		// This code is required to bypass ie6. bug "operations aborted"
		// You have to wait until onload in order to do document.body.appendChild which is a bug in Internet Explorer's implementation.
	 	if (window.addEventListener) window.addEventListener("load",buildMenus2008517817353,false);
        else if (window.attachEvent) window.attachEvent("onload",buildMenus2008517817353);
		//start creating menus
		var requestingFranchiseId = getRequestingFranchiseId2008517817353();
		var vehicleType = getVehicleType2008517817353();

		
			fetchAvailableYears2008517817353(requestingFranchiseId,vehicleType);
			fetchAvailableMakes2008517817353(requestingFranchiseId,vehicleType,'');
			fetchAvailableModels2008517817353(requestingFranchiseId,vehicleType,getMakeSelectedValue2008517817353(),'');
		
		
	}

	<script language="JavaScript" type="text/javascript">
		function subSort(fld){
			
				var str = fld.options[fld.selectedIndex].text;
				str = str.replace(/ \/ /gi,"/");
				var gaAction = str.replace(/ - /gi,"-") + '_Sort By';
				//alert(gaAction);
				pageTracker._trackEvent('Search Results Page', gaAction , 'Mainstage Header');
				globalTracker._trackEvent('Search Results Page', gaAction , 'Mainstage Header');
			
			document.location.href='index.cfm?action=inventorysearch&subaction=searchlist_gamma&bodycategory=Minivan&zipcode=77423&searchtype=bodytype&inventorytype=used&sendinfo=Submit&SortFilter=' + fld.value
		}
		
		function subRPP(fld){
			
				pageTracker._trackEvent('Search Results Page', fld.value + ' Items Per Page' , 'Mainstage Header');
				globalTracker._trackEvent('Search Results Page', fld.value + ' Items Per Page' , 'Mainstage Header');
			
			document.location.href='index.cfm?action=inventorysearch&subaction=searchlist_gamma&bodycategory=Minivan&zipcode=77423&searchtype=bodytype&inventorytype=used&sendinfo=Submit&ResultsPerPage=' + fld;
		}
		
	</script>

	<script language="javascript">

	function isValidEmail(anEmail){
		regEmail = /^[A-Za-z0-9\-_]+(\.[A-Za-z0-9\-_]+)*@([A-Za-z0-9\-_\.]+\.)+[A-Za-z]{2,3}$/i;
		return regEmail.test(anEmail);
	}
	function isValidZipCode(zipCode){
		zipPattern = /(^\d{5}$)/ ;
		return zipPattern.test(zipCode);
	}
	function validateGetOnlinePrice(thisForm){
		errors = "";
			errors += (thisForm.elements.gop_firstname.value.length < 2)?"\nFirst Name is required.":"";
			errors += (thisForm.elements.gop_lastname.value.length < 2)?"\nLast Name is required.":"";
			errors += (!isValidEmail(thisForm.elements.gop_homeemail.value))?"\nA valid email address is required.":"";
			isValidAreaCode = ((!isNaN(thisForm.elements.gop_homephonearea.value)) && thisForm.elements.gop_homephonearea.value.length == 3);
			isValidPhonePrefix = ((!isNaN(thisForm.elements.gop_homephoneprefix.value)) && thisForm.elements.gop_homephoneprefix.value.length == 3) ;
			isValidPhoneSuffix = ((!isNaN(thisForm.elements.gop_homephonesuffix.value)) && thisForm.elements.gop_homephonesuffix.value.length == 4);
		errors += (!isValidAreaCode || !isValidPhonePrefix || !isValidPhoneSuffix)?"\nA valid phone number is required.":"";
		//errors += (thisForm.elements.customerZipCode.value.length == 0)?"\nZip Code is required.":"";
			errors += (!isValidZipCode(thisForm.elements.gop_customerZipCode.value))?"\nA valid zip code is required.":"";

		if(errors.length){
			alert(errors);
			return false;
		} else{
			document.getonlineprice.submit();
			return true;
		}
	}
	
	function toggleGetOnlinePriceForm(make,model,yr,displayForm,inventoryid,bodystyle,stocknumber,type){
		document.getElementById('gop1yrmakemodeldiv').innerHTML = yr + ' ' + make + ' ' + model + ' ' + bodystyle;
		document.getElementById('gop1stocknumberdiv').innerHTML = 'Stock number ' + stocknumber;
		document.getElementById('gop2yrmakemodeldiv').innerHTML = yr + ' ' + make + ' ' + model + ' ' + bodystyle;
		document.getElementById('gop2stocknumberdiv').innerHTML = 'Stock number ' + stocknumber;
		
		if (document.getonlineprice.gop_make) document.getonlineprice.gop_make.value=make;
		if (document.getonlineprice.gop_model) document.getonlineprice.gop_model.value=model;
		if (document.getonlineprice.gop_year) document.getonlineprice.gop_year.value=yr;
		if (document.getonlineprice.gop_inventoryid) document.getonlineprice.gop_inventoryid.value=inventoryid;
		if (document.getonlineprice.gop_stocknumber) document.getonlineprice.gop_stocknumber.value=stocknumber;
			
		if (type == "gyop") {
			document.getElementById('HeaderDivID').innerHTML= "Get Your SmartChoice? Price";
			document.getElementById('InternalDivID').innerHTML= "We'll check to see if this vehicle is still in stock and provide you with pricing information--just give us your details.";
			document.getElementById('ConfirmationDivID').innerHTML= "Thank you for your inquiry! One of our friendly associates will be contacting you shortly with availability and pricing for this vehicle.";
			document.getonlineprice.gop_type.value = "gyop";
		}
		else 
			if (type == "check") {
				document.getElementById('HeaderDivID').innerHTML = "Check For More Discounts";
				document.getElementById('InternalDivID').innerHTML = "Provide your contact info to find out if you qualify for any additional discounts on this vehicle.";
				document.getElementById('ConfirmationDivID').innerHTML= "tpdata.SmartChoice.DiscountConfirmationText";
				document.getonlineprice.gop_type.value = "check";
			}
		
		if (displayForm == 1){
			document.getElementById("GetOnlinePriceFormSubmitted").style.display="none";
			document.getElementById("GetOnlinePriceForm").style.display="";
			mboxUpdate('AN_ADP_GetSmartChoicePrice','action=viewed');
			}
		else {
			document.getElementById("GetOnlinePriceFormSubmitted").style.display="";
			document.getElementById("GetOnlinePriceForm").style.display="none";
			}
		
		toggleFaderDiv('GetOnlinePriceContainer');
	}

	</script>

<script type="text/javascript" language="JavaScript">

function togglePricingLayer(){
	if (document.getElementById){
		if (document.getElementById("emailgate").style.display == ""){toggleFaderDiv("emailgate");}
		toggleFaderDiv("emailgate");
	}
}

function validatePriceDisplay(thisForm) {
		errors = "";
		errors += (!isValidEmail(thisForm.elements.emailbeforepricefield.value))?"\nA valid email address is required.":"";

		if(errors.length){
			alert(errors);
			return false;
		}else{
			return true;
		}
		
	}
</script>

	<script language="javascript">

		function validateQuickContactgmi(thisForm){
			errors = "";
			errors += (thisForm.elements.firstname.value.length < 2)?"\nFirst Name is required.":"";
			errors += (thisForm.elements.lastname.value.length < 2)?"\nLast Name is required.":"";
			errors += (!isValidEmail(thisForm.elements.homeemail.value))?"\nA valid email address is required.":"";
			isValidAreaCode = ((!isNaN(thisForm.elements.homephonearea.value)) && thisForm.elements.homephonearea.value.length == 3);
			isValidPhonePrefix = ((!isNaN(thisForm.elements.homephoneprefix.value)) && thisForm.elements.homephoneprefix.value.length == 3) ;
			isValidPhoneSuffix = ((!isNaN(thisForm.elements.homephonesuffix.value)) && thisForm.elements.homephonesuffix.value.length == 4);
			errors += (!isValidAreaCode || !isValidPhonePrefix || !isValidPhoneSuffix)?"\nA valid phone number is required.":"";
			//errors += (thisForm.elements.customerZipCode.value.length == 0)?"\nZip Code is required.":"";
			errors += (!isValidZipCode(thisForm.elements.customerZipCode.value))?"\nA valid zip code is required.":"";
			
			if(errors.length){
				alert(errors);
				//return false;
			} else{
				document.GetMoreInformation.submit();
				//return true;
			}
		}
	</script>

<script>
	function toggleGetMoreInformationForm(make,model,yr,bodystyle,stocknumber,vehicletype,vin,transmission,mileage,interiorcolor,exteriorcolor,askingprice,inventoryid,displayForm){
		document.getElementById("gmiyrmakemodeldiv").innerHTML = yr + " " + make + " " + model;
		document.getElementById("gmibodystylediv").innerHTML = bodystyle;		
		document.getElementById("gmistocknumberdiv").innerHTML = "Stock : " + stocknumber;
		
		document.GetMoreInformation.gmimake.value = make;
		document.GetMoreInformation.gmimodel.value = model;
		document.GetMoreInformation.gmiyr.value = yr;
		document.GetMoreInformation.gmibodystyle.value = bodystyle;
		document.GetMoreInformation.gmistocknumber.value = stocknumber;
		document.GetMoreInformation.gmivehicletype.value = vehicletype;
		document.GetMoreInformation.gmivin.value = vin;
		document.GetMoreInformation.gmitransmission.value = transmission;
		document.GetMoreInformation.gmimileage.value = mileage;				
		document.GetMoreInformation.gmiinteriorcolor.value = interiorcolor;
		document.GetMoreInformation.gmiexteriorcolor.value = exteriorcolor;
		document.GetMoreInformation.gmiaskingprice.value = askingprice;
		document.GetMoreInformation.gmiinventoryid.value = inventoryid;		
		
		if (displayForm == 1){
			document.getElementById("GetMoreInformationFormSubmitted").style.display="none";
			document.getElementById("GetMoreInformationForm").style.display="block";
			}
		else {
			document.getElementById("GetMoreInformationFormSubmitted").style.display="block";
			document.getElementById("GetMoreInformationForm").style.display="none";
			}
		
		toggleFaderDiv('getMoreInformationFormDiv');
	}
	
	</script>
